O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three sons, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine the fullness of it, and have finished for its exposings and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to my vision that I have fulfilled this with the cauterization, which is from hands' work, and it means "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is despised by all, if it is perished in the science and knowledge, and there is nothing left of the former that was written in books by the ancients, which the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and the vanity, and the intentions are closed and science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation; et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	I seem to think that I can revive this by putting the ordination of this cauterization according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation; and I will put together the forms of the fire-burning tools and other instruments of the work with the alignment of the declaration and preparation of it, as it is their craft.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no master of hands is found in our time, the art of medicine is extended.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters this to master the science of anatomy, as Galen says, so that he knows the judgment of the bones, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of parts, and has knowledge of the bones, nerves, teeth, and hairs, and the number of joints, and the movement and rest of the limbs, and the issue of the same.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc; et meismement en l’art de main.	And for this reason, Iocras says that the non and the evil are not with it, and with the hand is little; and at the same time in the art of the hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes; ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	In the introduction of this book, we say that who are not acquainted with things before said, if they go, they may err and mislead men; and I have often seen these who fall into this science and abandon the science and sense of experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col; por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	For I see a foolish man who cuts off my aposteme of scrophules or the col of a woman, and cuts the arteries of the col; for so much blood issues out that the woman dies in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans; si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	And see if another man who treated a piercing on a young man, the piercing was large; if it was taken out with a piece of the bladder, and he died in three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I have already been accused of the treatment, and see the position of the patient and the size of the piercing, and if it was well that it was cut, he died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie; et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine; et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie; et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	And see if another man who cured the duke of our land who had a broken leg, and with the splint on the wound; and the patients were ignorant and forced the fracture over the wound as soon as possible, and did not leave any mark on the wound, and left it eventually; and he commanded that it should not be removed; and later, when the leg was completely swollen and the wound was healed, it came to ruin.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe; et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	I am summoned to go to him, and I hurry to come and relieve his leg; and when I see it dislocated if it is in pain and does not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner; et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	However, all paths of the corrupted member were already confirmed or damaged, and could not be healed; and the corruption did not cease until the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And then another measure that would collapse the enchantment and then inflame due to the malice of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For gangrene, when it is free of melancholic matter, only then does one dare to touch it with iron if it is not in its part of the limb that can be completely healed what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions: c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions; et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	1. Therefore, thrice-wrought threads, you should know that handwork is divided into two parts: it is skill, whether or not there is danger in other arrangements; and I will show each part of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez; et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit; et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	1. Therefore, keep your hands safe so that they cannot be spoken ill of if you take up arms and armor lightly and firmly, and use the best way possible for the grace of God to come to your help and be strong; and let the unwholesome diseases of grief be healed; and guard your weapons from what makes you doubt, and have faith in yourself so that you can come out of this world with glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens: «Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	The Galenic doctors advise: "Do not take medicine for your illness, lest you become worse.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have found this treatment described in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez; et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	The first chapter is about fire cauteries and hot medicine cauteries, and it is the first chapter of the book from the chief to the feet; as well as the forms of strangulation, and of making incisions, and of all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses; et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	The second chapter is about cutting and piercing, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things; and it is the chapter ordered and the forms of strangulation.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses; et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things; and it is ordered by the loins' joints and the forms of the straps.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, let us remember our work, it is necessary that I give the quality of the help and not harm to each complexity.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus; et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu; et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	I say that the quality of the help and not harm is the longest word and subtle science and the secret remedy; and for this they speak more of the wounds, and agree on this; and they are short in their words because I do not trust the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions: c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	I say that cauterization helps universally with all complexions or matter, for whatever the complexion: it is to know complexion hot in matter, and complexion dry in matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide; et li autre dirent le contraire: que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	In hot and dry complexion, all matter is dissolved, and they say that cauterization is of no help; and the other says the opposite: that cauterization is only useful for diseases that come from choler and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour; et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	For the nature of fire is hot, and should not be curing hot diseases by choler, or for dryness; and those who say the opposite that cauterization helps greatly with hot diseases that come from the heart of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you perceive the chest of the patient and the heat to be on fire, you must cool the chest.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I concur with this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it once by experiment.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens; des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	And all ways, it does not interfere with anything except those who have experienced it and know the chapter of cauterizations, and the diversity of complexions of men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their seizures and spasms; other complexions do not have our pain, however, in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And they are ordered to resemble and correspond to the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that cauterization with fire is the secret of many remedies, and above all, it is a burning remedy.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and it only harms the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members in the slightest.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation; et par aventure ocit lou malaide Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The burning remedies come from one member to another by removing, and bring the maladies of grief to health; and by chance the patient Li feus for its highness and for the goodness of its substance does not harm, if it has no superfluity.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses; et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant; or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. And I found this in my experiments and through the long service and study I have given to this art, and it is true; and for this I apologize for the length of the words, as I only want to reveal the secret that is inside or fire, and the quality of the work, as it treats the diseases of the body, just as the philosopher says in demonstrating; and receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	1. Know, son, that the cauters should be made in such a way that they fit well and are not too tight.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere; et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	1. I say that the cauter is usable in all sizes because the wounds are not misplaced by the help of the cauter; and likewise, if the cauter is for necessary pains and hastans that cannot wait for the size that greatest malice does not come to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire; car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue; et il le dient ensi; mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	And never think that the fire cautery is harmful to the patient; for the disease that is cured by fire cautery has no return; and he tells him thus, but it is not so if he cares, because cauterization is only a medicine that dries the complexion and seizes the humors that cause pain, and is as good as medicine for hastening one's valor, and for one's virtue in one's work and signory.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut; et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie; mais ce avient poc.	And it is possible that the disease never returns according to the complexion of the patient and the lesion of the disease, and they are assembled in him by the acquisition of meat and other things, unless cauterization is administered to him or he has little excess and moisture, as for cauterization of deniers for pain, and the other things, and only some pain does not return; but this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir; mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	1. And many people do not understand why cauterization is called surgery by others, but it is seen; however, they only believe that cauterization is after medicine, but we understand it is false, and it is cauterization by surgery because when we administer remedies for any disease and they are not effective, then we apply cauterization, and it is effective.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	2. Therefore, it is well that cauterization is called surgery after medicine, but not according to the attention of the foolish.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance; et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes; et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	3. The ancients said that a golden cauterization instrument was as cruel as iron, and they said this because of the quality of the gold and its high substance; and they said that the golden cauterization did not cause any harm, but it is true because I have experienced it, and I found that it is true in some men; and golden cauterization is as cruel as iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez; et s’on le chaufe trop; si font au feu; et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	When you hold the gold instrument, you do not know when it is heated by the color of gold and has cooled down; and if it is heated too much, it melts; then it is enough to prevent it.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that's why we use fire cautery in our work, as we have found it to be effective.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or if you have commanded this chapter of the louse and flea bites, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	olive oil cautery
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	Olive oil cautery is used for moisture and cold in lice and fleas, and when it is done for the cause of a disease called "soda," and for many humors that descend from the head to the ears, eyes, and jaw, and for numerous sleeplessness, toothache, and gum pain, and for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, apoplexy, and semblances of diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir; et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	The form of this cauterization is if the patient is purged by a solvent medicine altering the third or fourth nut, according to which virtue and age and accustomed practice of the patient can endure; then repeat the dose for the patient's shoulder.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis; aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz; et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	Then place the palm of your hand between the roots of his palms between his two fingers; then if you have two means, if he bleeds, apply the olive oil which is called "olive" and is in this form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant; puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit; et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit; aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors; aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre; et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply ink to the joint, and descend and stretch your hand little by little, then loosen your hand, and reward the joint if you see the bone move slightly; and if you do not see it, continue the cauterization as long as you see the bone as I have told you; then take a piece of cloth, and soft cotton wool, and put it on the joint, and let it stay for three days; then apply moisturizing ointment called "tetrafarmaçon" until it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge; et por ce si aide mues.	And they said to the elder, that the more overgrown the wound is, the more it discharges; and for this reason, it helps to alleviate.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these say that too much hair should be cut off if part of the bone is also removed, and then remove what is bone from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors; et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte; aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	And they say that the cautery should be shaved as much as possible, and it must not be forced if it is large like the vertilus that women put in their wounds because the humors flow outside; and it must be shaved for a long time overgrown; afterward it must be treated and soothed.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor; et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier; car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres; et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	1. These two methods of cauterization do not seem less effective in general, regardless of whether or not one has fear; and it seems to me that I should leave them alone, as the head of the shoulder is often weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we have seen in other parts of the body; and even when the patient's strength is naturally weak, the first appearance of cauterization seems more salving and less painful to me, and I therefore use them accordingly.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	1. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres; et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	1. When the entire head is in chronic pain and lasts for a long time, if it must be used by the patient with pills and powders called "cochies," and purging of the head and oils and plasters; and when the cauterization is made as we have said before, it does not help.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit; adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	The patient's head is severely injured, and it cannot be moved; therefore, we cauterize a small part of it as we have mentioned earlier.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»; et est I leus en coi on met ventouses; et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os: li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors; et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	After cauterizing each corne of the head, as we have previously described, and then cauterizing the part called "vassels" or veins; it is placed in a vacuum; and tie your hand so that you do not see the bone: the patient feels too much pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will explain further; and it is necessary that the cauterizations of the corne be more subtle than those of the head's main vein, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	1. For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie: adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	2. For in one part of the fire cautery, there is sudden pain, and it spreads throughout the body, and the head is purged with medicines that change the oil, and all the other cures I have mentioned in the division of diseases are made, but none of them profit: therefore, I performed cauterizations in two ways, which is to say, with hot and dry medicine.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir; et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres; et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III; puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	3. If you apply hot and dry medicine to the cauterization, and it burns and causes the skin to peel and crust over, then make a temple out of the part where the pain is held in place so that you can pour in the plaster of Paris; and when it has been poured, let the lie and press it well and leave it for 12 hours; then remove it and apply the plaster of Paris, leaving the wound for 2 or 3 days; then make a cutting into the bursar as far as it presses in.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	After the cure of ointment as soon as it is healed; and if you see that there are no such medicines as I have written or dose treated of medicines.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The iron cauterization if it is according to this manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the cauterization of here is its form:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance; et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse; et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc. de la cure de fistule par cautere	The treatment of fistulas by cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere. Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, then continue the cauterization again once more, and if you are skilled at it, and leave it for three days; after that, put cotton wool in the bure, and apply the desiccating ointment as soon as it is dry, and when 40 days have passed and it is dry, if you put an acidic corrosive medicine on it, so that the bone is exposed; and then follow according to what you found in your chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient ones mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Understands the fistula, and puts in the forceps the subtle part of the cautery; then makes the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And they make it to the size of a .З. of plonc; and hold your hand on the cautery firmly, and do not move the patient until the ploncs are hard and do not come out of their oil; and it is necessary to put the oil in the clean linen pouch or in a small bottle: the ploncs if they are close to the fistula, and the healthy person will be safe.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the cauterization we have mentioned, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then it is necessary to administer emetine to the neck, and bring the fistula back to its original position according to what is appropriate for the patient's own throat.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times there are cracks in the lips that are called "cracks," and also in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have mentioned in divisions, and the patient does not benefit, then use a small cauterization tool according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And he places the head in those cracks as much as it fits; after curing the bone with cerate until it is sound.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the gallbladder
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When the gallbladder abscess comes from the root or the ureter, or the ducts, or the roots of the teeth, and it becomes infected and forms a fistule; and you cure it as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit much: therefore, it is necessary that you have a cauterization according to the size of the fistule; after the bite or rupture of the fistule, and hold your hand until the wound is healed, and then close it once or twice, after the cure of what we have said in the cures, as long as it is sound; and if it is cured once or twice, it is good; and if not, it is necessary to expose the bone and open the corrupt bone, according to what you will find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	The first sentence to translate is: "Ou cautere
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat them with medicines and it does not work, then put a bitter pill in your mouth; after that, wash the cautery that was formed thereafter in this manner, so that it looks like a dog's leash around the tooth; and remove the teeth from the cautery gently, and hold your hand tightly so that the patient feels the pain coming from the root of the tooth; after easing your hand and continue the cautery according to your will; after filling the patient's mouth with bitter water, and paint it once an hour and keep it fresh for a while.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in part, the teeth that were moving are confirmed, and the genital area becomes soft and restrained, and the moisture is corroded and dried out.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	When pain in the teeth comes from cold, or if it is cold or visible, and medical care is ineffective, then there is a need for cauterization in two ways: and cauterization with brimstone and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	Cauterization with brimstone if it is such that you prefer brimstone of sheep, and the end in a iron or steel fork; then take cotton and wrap it around the point of a pen, and make it with brimstone built, and place it on the painful tooth firmly and hold until it is cooled; and often I do this as long as the virtues reach the root of the tooth, and if you see that the linen and cotton in brimstone are burned, and place it on the painful tooth, and place iron chapt around it as much as the flesh reaches to the edge of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	1. When the fire cautery is used, if it is such that you ignite a piece of iron or steel, and it is large so that the flames do not reach the patient's mouth; then heat the cautery, and form it as follows, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery is cool; do this often because the pain will be eased for you or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	2. And it is necessary that the patient fills their mouth with hot blood in the pressure of this cautery, and then it becomes red; and this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	And make the burn as hot as you desire, according to what you can bear; and this is the shape of the cauterization:
des scrophules	of scrofulous boils
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the boils are fleabite and cold, and do not respond to digestion with medicines, then wash the cauterization tool with water after it comes into shape, and make openings for the smoke to escape from the other side; and put the cauterization tool on the abscess as many times as it can, until it is at the point of the abscess; and if the abscess is small, put the cauterization tool according to the amount of the abscess, and leave it for three days; and put cotton on it as it is sore; after that, cure the lesion with ointments and plasters as it is healthy.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the collar:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When moisture is present in the channels and at the same time when the face becomes cold, it is necessary that the patient be treated with soluble medicines first; after that, I perform a fire cautery at the base of the throat and tell you not to come too close to the throat and do not burn too much but only a little.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, I perform another cautery at the joint of the shoulder and call it the "clavicle" as we have mentioned before; and treat the limb as we have said as soon as it is healthy.
de la toust	Of the entire
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all the symptoms of measles are cold, and the patient has no fever, and it is an acute disease, then make incisions with the forceps on the sides; and the other cauterization is made between the two hams; and this is called the "clavicle" according to the form mentioned earlier.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never has it been adjusted to this nerve because it has eight burns.

Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated again, something happens quickly, therefore, perform cauterization on the large cauterization clavicle, or prick with cauteries.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is healed by moisture and is healthy for the patient.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains. For this reason, I made three burns on the heel of the foot due to the amount of a dose, at all the cauterization sites, and two burns to harden the two knees so that the cauterizations are at three angles, and they should be spaced apart between one and another so that they do not stick together as they sweat; and they should be like this so that they do not bite the two parts of the knee, and the figure of the cauterizations should be according to this form in an equal manner:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	2. dou cautere de pleuresin	3. And a cauterization of weeping

Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie. Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	However, in this case, there is no pain or the patient dies now, or a fistula comes that cannot be saved.
de la mice	of the mouse.

de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Fire cautery does not apply to dropsy, for it is called the "aplastic" method.
