de l’enfleure des piez	of the inflammation of the points
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the points are inflamed with water, and are hard like citrine, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the point between the ear and the anus; and gently hold the cauterization with the tool so as not to turn it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much into the forest, otherwise it will be harder to find one, and the fire cautery should be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making two cauteries on each leg at the point of the hoof; and let the cauteries be long enough to penetrate the sole of the foot, one in front and the other behind, along the leg; and leave the cauteries to heal for a long time after the cure is done; afterwards, the other cures that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the mustard
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and retentive virtues which are in the stomach and intestine are swollen, and cannot be cured by usual means; and you see the patient suffering greatly and of a green color, then make a fire cautery on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before or on the intestine, around the cauterization; and four cauteries should be made subtly at all the cauterization clavicles, and two cauteries on the hams.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	When you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then perform the cauterization on the point, and the cauterization on each side, and the punctures on the stomach, because the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are either fundament or several, and are old and large, and made up of cold and moist putrid humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit much if cauterization is done: III on should make an incision on the backbone, which is all deformed and broken in many places, and the cauterization on the bowels II times; and if you think that the stomach is cooled, and the meat is not cooked, and the face swells, then the face on the large cauterization on the stomach, as it is said before, and the other on the liver, and the other on the gallbladder at all the cauterizations; and leave the cauterization over long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the leg as much as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the chalcedony which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you touch hellul, if the cautery looks like a rasps, and then place it completely on the hellul coped; and leave as much of your hand as the cautery reaches to the vein's birth, without cutting; do this once or twice, and if it is lacking in hellul, cauterize each one as we have said; after treating wounds as much as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on alchatim, it will provide more help.
de plaie mal curee	Of a wound that was not treated properly
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure further treatment or opening, we will tell you in their case when they become seriously ill and cannot be healed by cauterization alone.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awakened and starts to produce sour milk and rotten moisture, if you provide it with total care and keep it at all times in the tent as it has, then you should guard the whole tent carefully.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the cauterization is washed and the bougie is placed in the fistula according to the amount of paste that entered, and the cauterization is resumed as long as the corns are sore and corrupted; once or twice, depending on the amount of ointment used; and warded off with a leather that has been cut, and large wounds.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	1. If the fistula is in the course of the ureter and the intestine, and you are sewing these loops, and do not perform this unless it is in the groin, and think that it is not a permanent solution; after healing the groin as much as possible, and if the loops are still present, and the materials are long and strong, then you can say that the groin is completely healed; and if the materials are not long and strong, say that the groin is torn, and corrupted the bone at its root; and then like one of these that we will say in his groin.
de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain in the head comes on suddenly, and with great wind, and no woman is near, then it is necessary that you burn it on both sides of the hair at the cauterization iron that we have mentioned before; and if we cauterize it in a moment, there will be three burns in line, and they will help greatly.
de la vessie	of the uterus
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the uterus is large and weak, and moist, if the midwife retains the urine, then you should burn it in the part of the hair that is near the uterus, either on the left or right side, and so that each cauterization is as far apart as one pace; and you should also cauterize the back of the uterus, or II may be too much; and so the cauterizations should be done according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marrows
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flow is corrupted and late; and when they come, it causes great pain: therefore, it is necessary to make three cauterizations along the belly, as we have said or cautery of the uterus, and second cauterization on the back; and if it is a cauterization of the clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the haunch
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the haunchbone, and for this reason if it is still in its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the limbs are in different departments, if it comes that you cauterize the patient on the haunchbone at the cautery point like a circle, and seignes before the knee on the haunch so that the haunchbone turns the circle; and if it is the cauterization such as those made on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, make three olive-sized cauterizations and they should be as large as the others; and the cure as soon as it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the back, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then it is necessary that you purge the patient of large amounts of fetid pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of cauterization is according to two methods: it is to know how to assemble burning medicines and cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	1. If the fire cautery is followed by various methods, then some are like this: you cauterize on the handle of the hazel according to this form, and make a good depth and thickness, and leave between each cauterization a space equal to a dozen, and it is olive oil; never once does one cauterize on the end of the hazel stem, because there are four according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	2. And if you see, if the cauterization is made on the circle we have mentioned in the dislocation of the hazel; but make it in part manner that the circles contain the whole hazel, and all its ends as they are.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is how one treats in sciatica, when the pain holds in the hip, and does not reach the thigh or the knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And when the pain reaches the thigh and the knee, one should cauterize there either the ankle or the malleolus IV times, on the side where there is less flesh; and whether it is the cutaneous or the espesseté dou keur cauterization, and if the patient feels that the pain spreads to two points or close to the cautery which is called "points", then it should be cauterized at those points.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is from the knee to the thigh, then cauterize with a circular or cutting cautery; and take good care of all your cauterizations so you don't burn the nerves and large arteries more than the cauterization, and do not cause further harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen others who cauterized on the ankle and caused pain that made the leg swell completely, the toe as well, and it was noticed and corroded in all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the belly where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts assembled, make a fire cautery on both, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And in the fire cautery of the thigh, at which they say, do it in this manner: make a piece of iron as follows, let it be as heavy as some large nut or less, and let it be divided into parts and let each part be divided into smaller pieces; let the divisions be equal to two parts, and let them be like noses, and have a handle of well-made iron; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be scraped as much as it is red and greasy-feeling, and then place it on the malleable shoulder of the patient, and bend it on the costeit; and the cautery is once reheated and left for three jors; and then apply ointment, and leave the wound open for a long time; after the cure of the ointment as much as it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use little of this cauterization because of the pain of the patient, and it is all that they can endure; and this is called burns, which they can bear, and later on, if they wish.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The ardent cauteries of medicine are those that you make and instruments with handles that enter the corner of the door, and are either of iron or of gold at one end, and in the middle have two pieces, and in the upper part have a quantity of the growth of a doe; and they are overturned and cut, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting the handle of the axe in the patient's grips, firmly press your hand on the handle; then grease between the two circles of the hot iron that is heated in the fire pit, and leave it for an hour, suffering the patient's pain and anxiety.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the cauterization is as if by fire; and when the cauterization has been removed, ease your hand with the instrument and raise the axe handle of iron soft, and leave it for three hours, and let it be as long as the black part of the bandage is osteit; and then leave three hours that the salve is straightened; and this will help after the care of wounds as soon as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain spreads to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that resembles what you have done in the hair; and this is the way of the hot tool, and I have written or described the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Prepare alkaline and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, and mix them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Or if there is a small hole that the tip of a razor cannot go through, and then pour it into another pot well-filled, and add alkaline and charcoal and soft ash, as much as you have two powders in your hand; and leave it until it drips water or can be poured, then take all this ash, and mix it with chalk and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	1. And when it is a matter of ague and the patient is in the state of mind of a novice in medicine and cauteries of other parts, then she will make an effort as if it were fire, and if other remedies are used such as well-applied hot iron, anacardium, and chalcedony with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	1. Galen relates a cure by which some were cured of the pain of the chilblain and sciatica, and he told us to follow this cure, and that it was completely cured in one case after performing this cure, and he was bathed in the same way as he instructed us afterward.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And then in another way, you should massage the affected area with fresh and dry vervain, and apply it to the shoulder, thigh, and leg where the pain is, and leave it for three hours and by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the pressure.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then I have it enter a bath as long as the chest is not raised, and then I have it enter a laxative, and the pain will disappear completely and it will be healthy.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	I advise that no one should use such a hot cauterizing medicine after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that if the sciatic nerve is cauterized with the hoof of a goat, it helps; and it must be done in a certain way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the linen and grease it slightly, then place it in the pouch that is between the little finger and the other, which is called the fascia.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After drying the goat's hoof and heating it until it is charred, and then placing it on the linen, and leaving it as long as there are stains; and repeat again, and continue until you think with your senses that it will reach the hip, and that the pain will cease; and this method of cauterization is called "cauterization with a goat's hoof.
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touch or percussion or from too much evacuation, or from the appearance of cold expanded matter, in none of these appearances is cauterization justified, rather it should be used on that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been cleansed of fetid pills or other appearances, that you cut on the back, where the pain remains, three lines marked with a line V, and in each line you cauterize or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear; and make the cauterization according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see, make III cauterizations or IV on the clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often affects many children, and the signs of its beginning are seen when they have their teeth tightened as they grow, and cry; and you see the spine bent double and the appearance that comes with the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe its cure, if it is burned at the cauterization point according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization turns purple in every part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if the cauterization is performed at the end of the spine at the point where it is pricked with two or three points, and they are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the wound as much as it is healthy according to what we have said, and warned that you should not perform a cauterization in gilberry that is in spam of the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints comes from moisture that is expanded to every member of the body, and when pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of cold cause and medicines do not cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: make a cut on the joint of the affected part, and if the cauterization is olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is your intention that you touch the face with long hair, then the cauterization is done all over the cauterization as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come to the joints and other joints, and it happens many times, then the cauterization is done on each knee III or IV of each part, all over the olive cauterization; and if you have skill for more, but do not hold your hand too long as much as the pain allows.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cauterization that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pain remains in the hands, then I make nine punctures along the line of the fingers; and if there is no more pain, then I make punctures at each joint and at the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes from the costal or shoulder blade, then cauterize each part and govern the patient's behavior with the physician and prescribe medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you govern his behavior and purge him of filth, then he will be cured by God.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rage of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When rage comes in wrath, and his brow hangs down and is new, then if you see that when you cure him he does not throw it away; and that he uses things that soften the stomach, so that he comes out of his stomach; after which you place it on his back between your hands, and command that he lick his hair as much as it is repaired, and draws it to your two hands, and signs with a sign that is like half of a circle around the curved bone, and in all signs that are like the half of a circle around the curved forehead; then wash the cauterization with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and has a slight moisture.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then smooth the bails on your leg; and the midwife stains her hand to make sure they do not return; she works well on the thighs of the patient, and puts the cautery sign on all her hands, and then puts it on the mark, and holds it firmly and as far as you can reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again until you touch the bone; and be careful that the bile does not rise when you make the cautery, that you do not burn it, and that neither the midwife nor any other midwife dies.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone at the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be done subtly according to the size of the bone, and also for adults according to their size; after three days, cure the leu of the wound as much as possible until the burn is healed; after the cure of other ointments as long as it is healthy, and gently put 40 jors on his back as long as the wound is well soaked; and it is necessary that the stitches be tightened for a long time, so that the exudate does not come out when he goes to bed in rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, he will find it difficult to stand, and after forty more days; and he should rest, so that he works quickly and does not have too much intoxication from drinking and eating, and does not have too high fever; and when he has completed this instruction, he is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the treatment of trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdomens and are known, and you see that they are not increasing, he should re-cautery according to the quantity, and so is the third angle of this form; after the treatment as we have said; and no of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized at a three-angle according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	1. But sign that the shoulder is healing and make a line for the widest part of the fracture, and another line for the narrowest, and hold your hand on all the cauterized clavicle.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	1. However, the first burns are less painful and more effective.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	2. of pain in no member.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	2. When pain comes in no member, either from chill or wound, and the pain lasts long, and medicine does not help, then it should be cauterized at the cauterization point called "points", and the cauterization should be according to the length of the member and its narrowness and its weakness and its location of torsions and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the patient is healthy after the first burn, that's good; if not, restart the burn at another spot, because it is customary for the patient to die at the part where the burn was applied, since it is necessary to perform the burns until the patient becomes healthy.
de meselerie	of medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The remedies are never helped by the burn once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the burning, when the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we said in the division, and not too soon or too late, and you doubt that corruption will spoil all the patient, then I make the following burns on the head: I cut off the hair, and the other on the forehead at the end of the curls; and they touch the corners, and the back to the hip; and it lasts as much as your hand that the burn lasts until the bone, and as much as the discharges issue forth so that the vapors of the large humors may issue forth; and I cauterize on the nails according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	1. If the wound is widespread; it is evident, if you cauterize it with these cauteries that we have mentioned or chief, and one cauterizes in general, and two cauteries are on the spine of the neck, and six cauteries are on the spine of the back, and the knuckles and the other fingers, and two cauteries are on the wrists and the ankles, and all the joints of the hands and feet, and the pits of the hands; and you will find nerves that are located below the shoulder blades, which are not burned, and no time has been made for a cauterization on the bone of the elbow, and the other on the stomach bone, and the other on the liver bone.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When you perform more cauterizations, the patient benefits more and does not feel pain in the cauterization if it is not as corrupt as the heart.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the wound with flour several times with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the cauterization is made on the member according to its size and thickness; and the treatment of ointments as soon as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	1. And no time is it done when cauterized and on the hand, wrist, and back, at the end of the nerve that is silent to the member, and if it is not flattened; and all this does not interfere with anything if one is not aware of the members and the movements of the forearms.
de albaras	2. Of scars
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	3. When the disease known as "scars" is aroused, and the art of medicine does not help, then cauterize with a cautery once every fortnight, according to the amount of the sweat, until the blister is ostee and turns red; then use flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and salves of colic and gout, for each part; and put all together, and bind with a bandage, and apply to the skin as often as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done with the cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the wise ones say that cauterization is also made in the circumference of the sore; and I think it is not very good because it may cause ulcers and corruption, and I have always wanted it to happen once; and the most appropriate thing is that it is cauterized around, with the cautery called "circular," as we have said in the past.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the tumor that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When some have a disease called 'adubelati', and it delays measuring either due to excessive production or because the patient's condition is too weak when they are old (i.e., very old), and they have little strength, or because of tightness; and you see it hesitating to measure: therefore, apply the cauterization by pricking with small cauterizing points; afterward, leave it alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hesitate to measure.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it hesitating at all the cauterization, if the cauterization is too hot, then the form of the cauterization is not correct.
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of these diseases called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization has perceived the heat, and it is such that the patient feels the cauterization in a way that the course of the urine is altered to some extent.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment when it is completely healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cauterization with fire by iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of disease called "corrodents" and it is nothing more than a rot of the limb, because it eats the limbs as it does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization with fire, then sharpen the cauterizations with small and large iron claws according to where the disease is; after cauterizing all parts as much as possible, and there will be nothing left of it, that everything that is corrupted is not osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on oiled bandages that cause burns with oil as long as the cauterized parts are still burning and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of ignited wounds with fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days there are no healthy burns being born, it is good; and if not, continue the cauterization on the parts that are still corrupting.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this disease has never been cured by medical treatment in the place of fire cauterization; but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said that the cure of the medical treatment in the division: take what you have in hand.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the porals that come to the piez
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it has happened that the piez was opened by accident due to a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that causes the piez to bend.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is known as fire cauterization, and hot iron cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is when you heat the iron until it glows like a torch, and it is made of red-hot iron according to the size of the nail that can be bent at all points, and has subtle margins; after that, you put the iron on the nail and turn your hand completely around the nail as it grows in the nail's root; then it leaves for three days until it starts to exude sweat; then I make a poultice of well-kneaded mud and leave it on all night, and the nails will be loosened from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the wound with ointment by rubbing it in as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they turn into deformed corpses, and many times appear in hands and fingers, then it is necessary that you perform a hot iron cautery; and in this way: take a nail or an iron pin, or a feather, and put it on the nail and the cloverleaf, which is to cover the warts; and then put the nail on so that it covers everything, then put a little hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn until the edge of the nail reaches the root of the cloverleaf, and it will find the hot water way perfectly shaped; and suffer the patient a little mordication of the hot water for an hour; then leave it alone, and it will fall off all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I make another after this, as long as you are careful of all these that are in the course, then I treat the wounds that engorge blood.
li cure dou trembler	it trembles
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If any tremble from cold or fever, or other, if it comes that you make four cauteries or four on the back, one cauterization between each spine; and one cauterization or a pinch, and on the stomach at the olive oil cautery; if it allows the trembling to cease, and the health improves from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	small pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	There is no instance where baths or pustules appear on the body, which come from large corrupting materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to cauterize them as soon as they appear, use a subtle cautery made of mirrite wood, or if the point is burned with fire, or the root of Aristolochia, or in a lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never are the cauterized ones made at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they do not grow new enqui forward, but are disordered by the superfluity that comes, and they are healthy; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the wound is closed
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there are great dislocations of blood from the wound that is closed at the incision or aphidiotomy, or fire cautery of the member, and similar things; and it is the worst thing to open.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And always when there is none, if you have to put your index finger at the vein wound, and press as much as possible until the vein is calmed by your index finger, and no more pain; then heat the olive-oil cauteries more often and larger so that they are all red; then I, or according to the size of the wound and the location of the leu, put the fire on the vein where the artery is located, and place the cautery at the vein where you hold your index finger, and hold the cautery until it is no longer painful.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If it jumps faster when you tie the vein with your other hand, and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another cautery that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue to do this one after the other until the nerve is no longer tight; and beware of burning the flesh that is red, and that no other malice comes upon the patient; and you should know that as soon as the artery is not dislocated, it cannot be well relieved immediately until the artery is large, if it is not by one of the four ways we have mentioned: either by cauterization or extraction when it is properly treated, or by gentle twisting of the thread, or by medicines applied which can cause relief from pain; and it should be tied and extracted.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will carefully maintain the ligature of threads or things burning on it, or other similar things, should not profit from it.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is none, and no remedy or medicine is present, then he must put his index on the wound of the vein as we have said, and firmly press until it is sore from the wound and the vein; and he should not move much, but often he must be cold, so that it does not freeze and become swollen and sore; and one should make inquiries beforehand about those who can cauterize and medicate.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	1. si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor. It only requires that you consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but put more caution in your honor than in your covenant, and do not believe everything, but rather what you are certain of and what you can have taken and lost; and use divination and indication in the cures of your diseases for the conversion of health; and this will help to this good reputation, glory, and memory.

dou chief plein d’aigue	A full-grown joint with inflammation.

de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the earwax
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses: ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer; ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois; ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	Everything that comes out of the ears is one of the four things: grains, stones, mineral points, or similar things; or seeds, like hazelnuts, feathers, peas; or something that flows, like acrid and ashy substances and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it comes out of the ear through the earhole or in any other way that does not fit well in the ear, and does not grow in the ear, then put the ear to the sun.

Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure; et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	This treatment often comes out once; and if it does not come out, then it is extracted with fine tweezers, and the form is like this:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin; se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure; et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne; puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit; et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor; puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	If it jumps out with tweezers, it is bad; if not, then extract with fine tweezers at the bone marrow of a small hole; and if it does not jump out, then make a loop of thread and cut the end of the cord or ear hole, and smoke it which is inside the ear wax if it comes in with the ear, then the treatment is formed, as we have said, if it does not come out in this way, then take some glue on the eyelids, and put in no instrument that can hurt it to make, and put a piece of cotton inside; then press the glue on the piercing or whatever it is, and extract.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme; et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant; et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche; et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If she does not jump from all these things that we have said, if you insist on pricking the ear even if it causes spasms, and the manner of pricking is to first use the blade of the scalpel on the temporal bone of the patient, according to the measure of its strength, then hold the blade between your hands and turn the ear towards the opposite side, and make a small cut at the root of the ear in the fat or where it depends; and let the cut be like a moon, as you go to the piercing, then the bone according to your strength, and the suction comes to your mouth; and the cure as soon as it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction; et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it is the grain that is in and it swells, then administer the extraction; and if it cannot be extracted, then administer the i spatumile tenve subtil according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces; puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	But do not cut too much when you think the grain is moist from the moisture of the ear, as long as you have done many pieces; then extract it with subtle pincers and saliva, as we have said, if the extractions are successful.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the ear, therefore, if the patient has a grain in the ear, then the midwife should use an esrnuement of condization first, and fill the ear with soft cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let it be known on this ear itself or where the fever is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps for this, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu; et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille; et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer; et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars; puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	If she does not jump, then take many piercings according to the length of your arm, and make them light; and put the herbs on one ear, and let it drip from there onto the other parts of your ear, and be careful with another hole in the ear that is in the ear; and continue to do this hole after hole until the fever is all gone, and when she jumps, all the fever is gone; and if you see, if you take one joint, and burn one of the joints in the ear, and the other joint hold in fire as much as the hotter joint is; then do another part of the joints as much as the fever is all gone, just like we said on the hole.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division; mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures; et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	In the removal of the tooth, if it is small in size, similar to a pea and a similar thing, it is treated as we have said in the division; but if it is large in size, it can be felt, which is the more delicate part to remove from the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil: s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	In the removal of the ears' jewelry, if you treat it as we have said in the division and use distillations, and the treatment does not profit, then look at the ear with the sun: if there are no holes, if you pull out the pliers gently, and if there are, then take the noose of this form:
